   function toggleCountries(){
        document.querySelector('#collapseCountries').classList.toggle('hidden')
        document.querySelector("#view-more").classList.toggle('hidden')
        document.querySelector("#view-less").classList.toggle('hidden')
        document.querySelector("#arrow-img").classList.toggle('transform')
        document.querySelector("#arrow-img").classList.toggle('rotate-180')
      }

      document.querySelector("#collapseCountriesBtn").addEventListener('click', function(event){
        toggleCountries()
      }, true);
  </script>

        s.async = true;
        s.src = 'https://widget.intercom.io/widget/' + window.intercomSettings.app_id;
        var x = d.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x);
      };
      if(w.attachEvent){w.attachEvent('onload', l);} else {w.addEventListener('load', l, false);}
    }
  })();
  </script>
  <script>
   window.siteUiConfig = {"nativeAppiFrame":false,"productClassification":null};
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var tabNodes = document.querySelectorAll('[data-tabs-btn]');

      tabNodes.forEach(function(node){
        node.addEventListener('click', handleTabClick);
      });

      function handleTabClick(e){
        if(this.classList.contains('active')){
          return;
        }
        hidePreviousTab().then(function(){
          var contentTab = document.getElementById(this.getAttribute('aria-controls'));
          this.classList.add('active');
          contentTab.classList.add('show');
          contentTab.classList.add('active');
        }.bind(this));
      }

      function hidePreviousTab(){
        return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
          tabNodes.forEach(function(node){
            if(node.classList.contains('active')){
              node.classList.remove('active');
              var contentTab = document.getElementById(node.getAttribute('aria-controls'));
              contentTab.classList.remove('show');
              setTimeout(function(){ // this delay is required for fade transition
                contentTab.classList.remove('active');
                resolve();
              }, 150);
            }
          });
        });
      }
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   document.addEventListener("touchstart", function(){
      }, false);

      function stopPropagationDropdown(){
        event.stopPropagation();
      }

      function closeAllDropdowns(){
        var dropdowns = document.querySelectorAll('.dropdown-js');
        dropdowns.forEach(function(node){
          node.setAttribute('aria-expanded', false);
          node.nextElementSibling.classList.remove('show');
        });
      }

      window.onclick = function(e){
        // close all dropdowns if not interacting with open dropdown
        if(!e.target.matches('.dropdown-js')){
          var dropdownMenu = e.target.closest('div.dropdown-menu');
          var li = e.target.closest('li.nav-item');
          if(dropdownMenu === null || li === null){
            closeAllDropdowns();
          }
        }
      }

      function dropdownClickHandler(e){
        var menu = e.target.nextElementSibling;
        if(menu.classList.contains('show')){
          menu.classList.remove('show');
          e.target.setAttribute('aria-expanded', false);
        } else {
          closeAllDropdowns();
          menu.classList.add('show');
          e.target.setAttribute('aria-expanded', true);
        }
      }

      function initDropdowns(){
        var dropdowns = document.querySelectorAll('.dropdown-js');
        dropdowns.forEach(function(node){
          node.addEventListener('click', dropdownClickHandler);
        });
      }

      function initHamburgerMenu(){
        var mainHamburgerMenu = document.getElementById('main-hamburger-menu');
        if(mainHamburgerMenu === null){
          return;
        }
        mainHamburgerMenu.addEventListener('click', function(){
          if(mainHamburgerMenu.classList.contains('active')){
            mainHamburgerMenu.classList.remove('active');
            document.querySelector('body').classList.remove('nav-open');
          } else {
            mainHamburgerMenu.classList.add('active');
            document.querySelector('body').classList.add('nav-open');
          }
        });
      }

      initDropdowns();
      initHamburgerMenu();
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   function checkForIncompatibleBrowsers(){
  if(navigator.userAgent.indexOf('MSIE') > -1){
    loadIncompatibleBrowserBanner('msie');
  } else if(navigator.userAgent.indexOf('UCBrowser') > -1){
    loadIncompatibleBrowserBanner('ucbrowser');
  } else {
    checkForOperaMiniDataSavingsMode();
  }
}

function checkForOperaMiniDataSavingsMode(){
  var isOperaExtreme = (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Opera Mini/') > -1) && (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Presto/') > -1);
  if(isOperaExtreme){
    loadIncompatibleBrowserBanner('opera_mini');
  }
}

function loadIncompatibleBrowserBanner(browser){
  if(window.XMLHttpRequest){
    xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
  } else {
    xhr = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
  }

  xhr.onreadystatechange = function(){
    if(xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200){
      var el = document.querySelector('body');
      el.innerHTML += xhr.response;
    }
  }

  // public.banners.incompatible_browser
  xhr.open("post", '/banners/incompatible-browser');
  xhr.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
  xhr.send('browser=' + browser);
}

checkForIncompatibleBrowsers(); // run on page load
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
